assert_distance_of_time_in_words(from, to=nil)

[ show source ]

    # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 21
21:   def assert_distance_of_time_in_words(from, to=nil)
22:     to ||= from
23: 
24:     # 0..1 with include_seconds
25:     assert_equal "less than 5 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 0.seconds, true)
26:     assert_equal "less than 5 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 4.seconds, true)
27:     assert_equal "less than 10 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 5.seconds, true)
28:     assert_equal "less than 10 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 9.seconds, true)
29:     assert_equal "less than 20 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.seconds, true)
30:     assert_equal "less than 20 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 19.seconds, true)
31:     assert_equal "half a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 20.seconds, true)
32:     assert_equal "half a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 39.seconds, true)
33:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 40.seconds, true)
34:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 59.seconds, true)
35:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 60.seconds, true)
36:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 89.seconds, true)
37: 
38:     # First case 0..1
39:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 0.seconds)
40:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 29.seconds)
41:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 30.seconds)
42:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.minutes + 29.seconds)
43: 
44:     # 2..44
45:     assert_equal "2 minutes", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.minutes + 30.seconds)
46:     assert_equal "44 minutes", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 44.minutes + 29.seconds)
47: 
48:     # 45..89
49:     assert_equal "about 1 hour", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 44.minutes + 30.seconds)
50:     assert_equal "about 1 hour", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 89.minutes + 29.seconds)
51: 
52:     # 90..1439
53:     assert_equal "about 2 hours", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 89.minutes + 30.seconds)
54:     assert_equal "about 24 hours", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
55: 
56:     # 1440..2879
57:     assert_equal "1 day", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
58:     assert_equal "1 day", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 47.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
59: 
60:     # 2880..43199
61:     assert_equal "2 days", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 47.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
62:     assert_equal "29 days", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 29.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
63: 
64:     # 43200..86399
65:     assert_equal "about 1 month", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 29.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
66:     assert_equal "about 1 month", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 59.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
67: 
68:     # 86400..525599
69:     assert_equal "2 months", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 59.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
70:     assert_equal "12 months", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.years - 31.seconds)
71: 
72:     # 525600..1051199
73:     assert_equal "about 1 year", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.years - 30.seconds)
74:     assert_equal "about 1 year", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.years - 31.seconds)
75: 
76:     # > 1051199
77:     assert_equal "over 2 years", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.years + 30.seconds)
78:     assert_equal "over 10 years", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.years)
79: 
80:     # test to < from
81:     assert_equal "about 4 hours", distance_of_time_in_words(from + 4.hours, to)
82:     assert_equal "less than 20 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from + 19.seconds, to, true)
83:   end

1182: 
1183:     expected = %{<select id="post_written_on_1i" name="post[written_on(1i)]">\n}
1184:     expected << %{<option value="1999">1999</option>\n<option value="2000">2000</option>\n<option value="2001">2001</option>\n<option value="2002">2002</option>\n<option value="2003">2003</option>\n<option value="2004" selected="selected">2004</option>\n<option value="2005">2005</option>\n<option value="2006">2006</option>\n<option value="2007">2007</option>\n<option value="2008">2008</option>\n<option value="2009">2009</option>\n}
1185:     expected << "</select>\n"
1186: 
1187:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]">\n}
1188:     expected << %{<option value="1">January</option>\n<option value="2">February</option>\n<option value="3">March</option>\n<option value="4">April</option>\n<option value="5">May</option>\n<option value="6" selected="selected">June</option>\n<option value="7">July</option>\n<option value="8">August</option>\n<option value="9">September</option>\n<option value="10">October</option>\n<option value="11">November</option>\n<option value="12">December</option>\n}
1189:     expected << "</select>\n"
1190: 
1191:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_3i" name="post[written_on(3i)]">\n}
1192:     expected << %{<option value="1">1</option>\n<option value="2">2</option>\n<option value="3">3</option>\n<option value="4">4</option>\n<option value="5">5</option>\n<option value="6">6</option>\n<option value="7">7</option>\n<option value="8">8</option>\n<option value="9">9</option>\n<option value="10">10</option>\n<option value="11">11</option>\n<option value="12">12</option>\n<option value="13">13</option>\n<option value="14">14</option>\n<option value="15" selected="selected">15</option>\n<option value="16">16</option>\n<option value="17">17</option>\n<option value="18">18</option>\n<option value="19">19</option>\n<option value="20">20</option>\n<option value="21">21</option>\n<option value="22">22</option>\n<option value="23">23</option>\n<option value="24">24</option>\n<option value="25">25</option>\n<option value="26">26</option>\n<option value="27">27</option>\n<option value="28">28</option>\n<option value="29">29</option>\n<option value="30">30</option>\n<option value="31">31</option>\n}

1411:     expected << "</select>\n"
1412: 
1413:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]">\n}
1414:     expected << %{<option value="1">January</option>\n<option value="2">February</option>\n<option value="3">March</option>\n<option value="4">April</option>\n<option value="5">May</option>\n<option value="6" selected="selected">June</option>\n<option value="7">July</option>\n<option value="8">August</option>\n<option value="9">September</option>\n<option value="10">October</option>\n<option value="11">November</option>\n<option value="12">December</option>\n}
1415:     expected << "</select>\n"
1416: 
1417:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_3i" name="post[written_on(3i)]">\n}
1418:     expected << %{<option value="1">1</option>\n<option value="2">2</option>\n<option value="3">3</option>\n<option value="4">4</option>\n<option value="5">5</option>\n<option value="6">6</option>\n<option value="7">7</option>\n<option value="8">8</option>\n<option value="9">9</option>\n<option value="10">10</option>\n<option value="11">11</option>\n<option value="12">12</option>\n<option value="13">13</option>\n<option value="14">14</option>\n<option value="15" selected="selected">15</option>\n<option value="16">16</option>\n<option value="17">17</option>\n<option value="18">18</option>\n<option value="19">19</option>\n<option value="20">20</option>\n<option value="21">21</option>\n<option value="22">22</option>\n<option value="23">23</option>\n<option value="24">24</option>\n<option value="25">25</option>\n<option value="26">26</option>\n<option value="27">27</option>\n<option value="28">28</option>\n<option value="29">29</option>\n<option value="30">30</option>\n<option value="31">31</option>\n}

test_date_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2315
2315:   def test_date_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2316:     @post = Post.new
2317:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2008, 7, 16, 23, 30)
2318: 
2319:     options = {
2320:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2321:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2322:       :discard_type => false,
2323:       :include_blank => false,
2324:       :ignore_date => false,
2325:       :include_seconds => true
2326:     }
2327:     date_select(@post, :updated_at, options)
2328: 
2329:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2330:     #       don't change this!
2331:     assert_equal({
2332:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2333:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2334:       :discard_type => false,
2335:       :include_blank => false,
2336:       :ignore_date => false,
2337:       :include_seconds => true
2338:     }, options)
2339:   end

test_datetime_select_discard_month()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2118
2118:   def test_datetime_select_discard_month
2119:     @post = Post.new
2120:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2004, 6, 15, 15, 16, 35)
2121: 
2122:     expected = %{<select id="post_updated_at_1i" name="post[updated_at(1i)]">\n}
2123:     1999.upto(2009) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{i}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 2004}>#{i}</option>\n) }
2124:     expected << "</select>\n"
2125:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_updated_at_2i" name="post[updated_at(2i)]" value="6" />\n}
2126:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_updated_at_3i" name="post[updated_at(3i)]" value="15" />\n}
2127: 
2128:     expected << " &mdash; "
2129: 
2130:     expected << %{<select id="post_updated_at_4i" name="post[updated_at(4i)]">\n}
2131:     0.upto(23) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 15}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
2132:     expected << "</select>\n"
2133:     expected << " : "
2134:     expected << %{<select id="post_updated_at_5i" name="post[updated_at(5i)]">\n}
2135:     0.upto(59) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 16}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
2136:     expected << "</select>\n"
2137: 
2138:     assert_dom_equal expected, datetime_select("post", "updated_at", :discard_month => true)
2139:   end

test_datetime_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2341
2341:   def test_datetime_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2342:     @post = Post.new
2343:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2008, 7, 16, 23, 30)
2344: 
2345:     options = {
2346:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2347:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2348:       :discard_type => false,
2349:       :include_blank => false,
2350:       :ignore_date => false,
2351:       :include_seconds => true
2352:     }
2353:     datetime_select(@post, :updated_at, options)
2354: 
2355:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2356:     #       don't change this!
2357:     assert_equal({
2358:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2359:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2360:       :discard_type => false,
2361:       :include_blank => false,
2362:       :ignore_date => false,
2363:       :include_seconds => true
2364:     }, options)
2365:   end

2281:     expected << "</select>\n"

2416:   def test_select_datetime_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2417:     options = {
2418:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2419:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2420:       :discard_type => false,
2421:       :include_blank => false,
2422:       :ignore_date => false,
2423:       :include_seconds => true
2424:     }
2425:     select_datetime(Time.now, options)
2426:

2428:     #       don't change this!
2429:     assert_equal({
2430:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2431:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },

test_select_time_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2439
2439:   def test_select_time_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2440:     options = {
2441:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2442:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2443:       :discard_type => false,
2444:       :include_blank => false,
2445:       :ignore_date => false,
2446:       :include_seconds => true
2447:     }
2448:     select_time(Time.now, options)
2449: 
2450:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2451:     #       don't change this!
2452:     assert_equal({
2453:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2454:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2455:       :discard_type => false,
2456:       :include_blank => false,
2457:       :ignore_date => false,
2458:       :include_seconds => true
2459:     }, options)
2460:   end

1535:

1537:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]" value="6" />\n}

1539:

1547:

1549:   end
test_time_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2367
2367:   def test_time_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2368:     @post = Post.new
2369:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2008, 7, 16, 23, 30)
2370: 
2371:     options = {
2372:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2373:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2374:       :discard_type => false,
2375:       :include_blank => false,
2376:       :ignore_date => false,
2377:       :include_seconds => true
2378:     }
2379:     time_select(@post, :updated_at, options)
2380: 
2381:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2382:     #       don't change this!
2383:     assert_equal({
2384:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2385:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2386:       :discard_type => false,
2387:       :include_blank => false,
2388:       :ignore_date => false,
2389:       :include_seconds => true
2390:     }, options)
2391:   end

test_time_select_with_html_options_within_fields_for()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 1608
1608:   def test_time_select_with_html_options_within_fields_for
1609:     @post = Post.new
1610:     @post.written_on = Time.local(2004, 6, 15, 15, 16, 35)
1611: 
1612:     fields_for :post, @post do |f|
1613:       concat f.time_select(:written_on, {}, :class => 'selector')
1614:     end
1615: 
1616:     expected = %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_1i" name="post[written_on(1i)]" value="2004" />\n}
1617:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]" value="6" />\n}
1618:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_3i" name="post[written_on(3i)]" value="15" />\n}
1619: 
1620:     expected << %(<select id="post_written_on_4i" name="post[written_on(4i)]" class="selector">\n)
1621:     0.upto(23) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 15}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
1622:     expected << "</select>\n"
1623:     expected << " : "
1624:     expected << %(<select id="post_written_on_5i" name="post[written_on(5i)]" class="selector">\n)
1625:     0.upto(59) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 16}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
1626:     expected << "</select>\n"
1627:
